			function setRedirectCookie() {
				let monthInSeconds = 30 * 24 * 60 * 60;
				document.cookie = `_rotz=1; domain=zoznam.sk; Max-Age=${monthInSeconds}`;
				document.cookie = `_rotz_updated=1; domain=zoznam.sk; Max-Age=${monthInSeconds}`;
			}
			if(document.cookie.match(/_rotz=1/)) {
				if(!document.cookie.match(/_rotz_updated=1/)) {
					setRedirectCookie();
				}
				document.location = 'https://stary.zoznam.sk/'
			}

<script>
	var store = window.localStorage || {};

	$(".services-all").click(function() {
		$(this).toggleClass( "show-less" );
		if($(this).text() === "Zobraziť všetky služby") {
			$(this).text("Zobraziť menej");
			store.setItem('services.expand', '1');
		} else {
			$(this).text("Zobraziť všetky služby");
			store.setItem('services.expand', '0');
		}
		$(".services-list .hidden").toggleClass( "is-visible" );
	});
	if(store.getItem('services.expand') === '1') $(".services-all").click();

	$.getJSON('https://kariera.zoznam.sk/top_companies.php', function(json) {
		var imgTemplate = '<a href=""><img src="" alt=""></a>';
		var $topCompanies = $('#top_companies');
		shuffleArray(json);
		json.forEach(function(item, index) {
			if(index > 1) return false;
			var $a = $(imgTemplate);
			var $img = $a.children().first();
			$a.attr({ href: item.url });
			$img.attr({ src: item.img, alt: item.name });
			$topCompanies.append($a);
		});
		$('#top_companies_container').show();
	});
	function gotoKariera() {
		window.open('http://kariera.zoznam.sk/pracovne-ponuky/'+$('#cat').val()+'/'+$('#loc').val()+'#utm_source=zoztitulka', "TitulkaKariera");
		return false;
	}
</script><section class="box-section big-triple gtm_domace" >

<template id="vue-component-settings-box">
	<div class="modal-box-overlay" ref="modal-box">
		<div @click.self="close" class="modal-box-overlay-content" ref="modalContentBox">
			<div class="modal-box-settings">
				<h2>{{ box.title }}</h2>
				<button class="close" @click="close"></button>
				<div class="modal-box-settings-option clearfix">
					<div v-for="(item, index) in options" :class="'setting-' + box.type">
						<input v-if="box.type === 'radio'" :id="'modal-item-'+index" @click="box.selected = getFormat('value', item); save();" type="radio" name="modal-item" :value="item" :checked="getFormat('value', item) === selected">
						<input v-else :id="'modal-item-'+index" v-model="box.selected" type="checkbox" :value="getFormat('value', item)">
						<label :for="'modal-item-'+index">{{ getFormat('name', item) }}</label>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div v-if="box.type !== 'radio'" class="setting-button">
					<button @click="save">Nastav</button>
				</div>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>
</template>
<script>
	Vue.component('settings-box', {
		template: '#vue-component-settings-box',
		props: ['selected', 'title', 'options', 'type', 'format'],
		data: function() {
			return {
				box: {
					hasFormat: (this.format && typeof this.format === 'object' && this.format.name && this.format.value),
					title: this.title,
					options: this.options,
					type: this.type,
					selected: this.selected,
				},
			};
		},
		methods: {
			getFormat: function(what, object) {
				if(!this.box.hasFormat) return object;
				return what === 'name' ? object[this.format.name] : object[this.format.value];
			},
			save: function() {
				this.$emit('change', this.box.selected);
			},
			close: function() {
				this.$emit('close', this.box.selected);
			}
		}
	});
</script>
